SHX_great_game = {
    SHX_establish_rk_KOR = {
	icon = generic_prepare_civil_war

		highlight_states = {
			highlight_state_targets = {
				state = 525
				state = 527
				state = 1345
				state = 1346
				state = 1347
			}
			highlight_color_while_active = 3
			highlight_color_before_active = 2
		}

	available = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				KOR = { exists = yes }
			}
			KOR = { is_subject_of = SHX }
		}
		525 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = SHX is_subject_of = SHX } } }
		527 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = SHX is_subject_of = SHX } } }
		1345 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = SHX is_subject_of = SHX } } }
		1346 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = SHX is_subject_of = SHX } } }
		1347 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = SHX is_subject_of = SHX } } }
		OR = {
				525 = { NOT = { is_core_of = SHX } }
				527 = { NOT = { is_core_of = SHX } }
				1345 = { NOT = { is_core_of = SHX } }
				1346 = { NOT = { is_core_of = SHX } }
				1347 = { NOT = { is_core_of = SHX } }
		}
	}

	fire_only_once = yes

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 5
	}
	complete_effect = {
		KOR = {
			every_core_state = {
				remove_core_of = KOR
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_claimed_by = KOR
				}
				remove_claim_by = KOR
			}
		}
		525 = { add_core_of = KOR }
		527 = { add_core_of = KOR }
		1345 = { add_core_of = KOR }
		1346 = { add_core_of = KOR }
		1347 = { add_core_of = KOR }
		release = KOR
		KOR = { 
			every_core_state = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						NOT = { 
							is_core_of = SHX
						}
						OR = {
							is_owned_by = SHX
							OWNER = { is_subject_of = SHX} 
						}
					}
				}
				transfer_state_to = KOR
			}
		}
		KOR = { 
			set_cosmetic_tag = SHX_KOR_OCC
			load_focus_tree = generic_focus            

			create_country_leader = {
				name = "National Army Administration"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/WDSHX/China_Cross_leader.png"
				expire = "1.1.1"
				ideology = christian_socialism_subtype
				traits = {
				}
			}

			SHX = {
				set_autonomy = {
					target = KOR
					autonomous_state = kx_colored_puppet
				}
			}

			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = radical_socialist
				elections_allowed = no
			}


			set_popularities = {
				syndicalist = 20
				social_democrat = 20
				radical_socialist = 60
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = radical_socialist
				name = "National Army Administration"
				long_name = "National Army Administration"
			}
		}
	}
}

		688 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = SHX is_subject_of = SHX } } }
		901 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = SHX is_subject_of = SHX } } }
		OR = {
				301 = { NOT = { is_core_of = SHX } }
				688 = { NOT = { is_core_of = SHX } }
				901 = { NOT = { is_core_of = SHX } }
		}
	}

	fire_only_once = yes

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 5
	}
	complete_effect = {
		PAR = {
			every_core_state = {
				remove_core_of = PAR
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_claimed_by = PAR
				}
				remove_claim_by = PAR
			}
		}
		301 = { add_core_of = PAR }
		688 = { add_core_of = PAR }
		901 = { add_core_of = PAR }
		release = PAR
		PAR = { 
			every_core_state = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						NOT = { 
							is_core_of = SHX
						}
						OR = {
							is_owned_by = SHX
							OWNER = { is_subject_of = SHX} 
						}
					}
				}
				transfer_state_to = PAR
			}
		}
		PAR = { 
			set_cosmetic_tag = SHX_PAR_OCC
			load_focus_tree = generic_focus            

			create_country_leader = {
				name = "National Army Administration"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/WDSHX/China_Cross_leader.png"
				expire = "1.1.1"
				ideology = christian_socialism_subtype
				traits = {
				}
			}

			SHX = {
				set_autonomy = {
					target = PAR
					autonomous_state = kx_colored_puppet
				}
			}

			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = radical_socialist
				elections_allowed = no
			}


			set_popularities = {
				syndicalist = 20
				social_democrat = 20
				radical_socialist = 60
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = radical_socialist
				name = "National Army Administration"
				long_name = "National Army Administration"
			}
		}
	}
}

SHX_establish_rk_URG = {
	icon = generic_prepare_civil_war

		highlight_states = {
			highlight_state_targets = {
				state = 300
			}
			highlight_color_while_active = 3
			highlight_color_before_active = 2
		}

	available = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				URG = { exists = yes }
			}
			URG = { is_subject_of = SHX }
		}
		300 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = SHX is_subject_of = SHX } } }
		OR = {
				300 = { NOT = { is_core_of = SHX } }
		}
	}

	fire_only_once = yes

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 5
	}

			every_core_state = {
				remove_core_of = URG
			}
			every_state = {

					is_claimed_by = URG
				}
				remove_claim_by = URG
			}
		}
		300 = { add_core_of = URG }
		release = URG
		URG = { 
			every_core_state = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						NOT = { 
							is_core_of = SHX
						}
						OR = {
							is_owned_by = SHX
							OWNER = { is_subject_of = SHX} 
						}
					}
				}
				transfer_state_to = URG
			}
		}
		URG = { 
			set_cosmetic_tag = SHX_URG_OCC
			load_focus_tree = generic_focus            

			create_country_leader = {
				name = "National Army Administration"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/WDSHX/China_Cross_leader.png"
				expire = "1.1.1"
				ideology = christian_socialism_subtype

				}
			}

			SHX = {

					autonomous_state = kx_colored_puppet
				}
			}

			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = radical_socialist
				elections_allowed = no
			}


			set_popularities = {
				syndicalist = 20
				social_democrat = 20
				radical_socialist = 60
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = radical_socialist
				name = "National Army Administration"
				long_name = "National Army Administration"
			}
		}
	}
